<Rating>5</Rating><date>1594626942767< /date><Text>I can't put into words how excited I am to finally have a legit Halal (certified) American burger/diner food option, here in the Concord area.

Prior to this place opening; For years, we had to travel to places like Mirchi's in Dublin, Falafel Corner in Fremont, or Q's Halal Chicken in Alameda/Richmond.

I had always hoped that a place that offered high-quality, restaurant-oriented, American/Afghan fusion-food would come to Concord, but I wasn't sure if/when, it would happen.

This place has some of the best halal cheeseburgers I've ever tasted, and is definitely on-par  (the same standard of amazing quality) that is found in Fremont, Dublin, and all the other places in the South Bay.

Extremely delectable bacon & beef patties, smothered with American cheese, a toasted bun, and all the right sauces. Their Chicken Quesadilla & Philly Gyro, are made with succulent & tender halal meat.

There is another Falafel Flame location in Dublin, which too is also amazing, but this place is identical in its superb quality & ingredients, but so much closer to residents of Concord/Walnut Creek.

My favorites definitely have to be the Hawaiian Burger, BBQ Chicken Wings, Philly Gyro Wrap, Curly Fries, and Chicken Quesadilla.

I hope this location can start offering halal pizza in the near future, as well.

Now all we need is a Halal Chinese/Halal Mexican restaurant in Concord, and we will be on-par with our fellow kindred in Fremont & the South Bay Area.<//Text><Name>David A.<//Name><GmapID>0x8085674761c9c8f7:0xaea82a13ccf2920e<//GmapID><resp>None< /resp>< pics>

< Rating>
4</Rating>
< Review>
Any breakfast place that has biscuits and Gravy on their menu would automatically be a 4-star experience for me. Granted, Big Daddy's definitely serving up some good grub. Having lived in Sonoma County for practically all my life I've been around the block a time or two and when it comes to breakfast this diner is holding steady.

The breakfast here is superb and you can't go wrong with simple items such as pancakes, eggs, potatoes, and a variety of bread slices. The burrito is a pleasant surprise and as I raved before their sausage gravy is pretty darn good. I've never had dinner at this establishment but there lunch seems to hold it's own as well.

Big daddy... I'll be back.</Review>

Food was bland. Corned beef hash had no salt and potatoes were not cooked. Hollandaise tasted like butter, nothing else. Home fries were okay, but on my last bite, I bit down on something hard. Upon examining the object I hit down on, I discovered it to be a piece of hard black plastic. There were several other pieces in the bite I spit out. My tooth is still hurting. I let the waitress know and she  came back, said nothing, and left the revised check. We paid in full for the meal and tipped despite the generosity. I let the other waitress know that we were not trying to get out of paying for the meal, that we were concerned that there may be something that got into the food. She claimed that it was probably pepper. I told her that I tasted it and assured her that it was NOT pepper. It was hard plastic or other material that was not food. I gave them two samples of broken scrap that I pulled from my mouth, not that I wanted them to touch them, but maybe they can identify what it was. They just didn't care. Never going back.<//review>

<review>I enjoy a dive diner every once in a while, having eaten here once before, I thought I'd try it again, I know realize why I haven't been back in ages. Sadly, this place is more dilapidated and filthy than was acceptable. The outside tables have paint chipping off of them, the service was incredibly slow considering 90% of the tables were empty and those with patrons were already served. The food was bland, however the oil used tasted stale and old. While the eggs were prepared appropriately, they were heavily salted, the ham was the consistency of rubber, the hashbrowns had that stale old oil flavor, but more than anything the place feels as if it hasn't been cleaned in over a decade, the place is beat up, and it shows. The bathrooms were covered in grime, the floors were covered in grime. I can't believe the Health Department doesn't shut this place down. There are far better places to eat in Sonoma County, how this one stays open is beyond me.</review>< pictures>

Finally got to visit this awesome place on Friday May 18, 2018, at 830PM.

It was a friend's birthday and I'd seen how often she partied here, so I had to check it out.

The corner location makes it easy to find, with ample street parking (as their lot is pretty small). Luckily I had no issues finding a spot right at front entrance.
Arrive early to get a good & safe spot.

Bouncers outside and inside. 21+.
That night was $10 cover, CASH.
(tho I'm told this is the norm)

A dance room with Dj & Live bands.
And a karaoke room with Dj too. It's a great ambiance overall, very relaxed.

Plenty food choices & decent prices
(See menu pics). I picked the jalapeno poppers, cheese sticks, and steak fries, all were delish! Plastic accepted.

Waiters were friendly & attentive,
tho a bit pushy to get you to buy more.
I say this bc due to cover charge,  there aren't drink minimums.

Karaoke Dj was good, he jammed out
to a few songs, a bit picky about
PEOPLE SINGING W DRINK IN HAND.
(He takes a photo of EVERY singer).

Mostly 80s songs, divey, fun crowd...
Starts slow,  but does fill up!!

Enjoy the photos. Like the review.

Recommended.<//text>
< user_name>
Ely Diaz<//user_name>

<rating>4</rating><Text>Came on a night with a tribute band and karaoke and boy, was it busy (and loud)! Cash-only cover charge.

Karaoke room was really supportive of everyone who went up and sang along for crowd favorites. Mics worked pretty well and there TONS of lyrics screens so you can look around the room more.

Major complaint is they won't serve you a glass of water, even if you order a drink. Seriously management?? Take care of your customers! I need at least one glass of water per alcoholic drink, so if you can't give me some free tap water, i just won't buy drinks.

Drinks and food were pretty decent. Fast drink service despite the crush.

An excessively drunk guy kept making a scene and getting in people's space and i wish security would have done something, but he wasn't belligerent --- just overly party-happy.

< text>
At first glance. It looks like your typical dive bar.  That in itself can either be intimidating or off putting to some. I personally find this place to be more like a hidden gem. The experience here varies on the times you go. I enjoy going after work with friends sitting at the bar and having a few drinks. The place offers Karaoke for those who love to swoon. They have bands that come through some times and also offer dancing on certain days. What I mostly enjoy about this place is the food. You would never suspect the food is any good here but I promise you their food cannot be missed. Order their burgers and you will taste or smell nothing better. A burger that smells better with every bite taken is a riddle to me but one that I enjoy every time I go. Also their wing appetizers are amazingly good and sharable. The staff are all amazing, friendly and helpful. This is definitely a place I recommend to people.</text>

All my favorite bands from the 80's that I didn't get to see, I can see at New Wave bar. From the Flock of Seagulls to Missing Persons, I have gotten to see up close the bands I missed so long ago. It continually thrills me that they can get these big names to come to a bar. I can see and hear them up close and personal. Some of the instruments they used in the 80's I was unsure of, but when they play at New Wave bar, I can see the instruments they used. The most surprising was Flock of Seagulls which I was certain they used instruments that maybe I have never seen, but the talent they display with a synthesizer and two guitars and a drummer just still blow me away. Thank you New Wave bar. PS. you can meet the band usually right outside the door and lavish your praises on a personal level.< /Review>

Stephanie Han<//username>
<Date>1412614434946< /Date>< Rate>
4<//Rate>
<review>My friends and I came here to see Flashpants a few weeks ago and had a blast! The place had been on our radar for quite a while but it just took us a while to get it together. The cover is $5 til 8pm, $10 after, which I didn't think was too bad for going to see a band. The place is quite roomy, with 80s paraphernalia everywhere. Loved seeing all the vintage 12" LP covers of all my favorite bands. They have two main areas: the stage and dance floor, and a side dining/lounging area, which could use a little more style, but was all right. When we got there around 9pm there were plenty of tables available but they do fill up fast. We saw a person walk by with this giant glass orb drink and found out it was called "The Fish Bowl," and we knew we had to get it! It's definitely big enough to share, and bonus points for the flashing light floating around in it as well!

The band went on stage around 10pm and played for at least a couple of hours, with a short break in between. They were hilarious! I'd caught them at a free performance at a Movies on the Beach and they did not disappoint. If anything, since this was an adults-only club their antics were crazier and funnier. The crowd is on the older side, definitely playing on the mostly Gen Xers' nostalgia. A LOT of bday celebrations going on--apparently if you're over the age of 40 this is the place, lol. Anyhoo, a good time had by all, and we're looking forward to catching one of the many 80s tribute bands that come through here on a regular basis.</review>< pictures>
